[05:22:01 PM CT] [Email Feed] Austin Holland
    For deploying OpenEMR on Azure, the Azure App Service (PaaS) is generally the most affordable and easiest to manage, while an Azure VM (IaaS) offers the highest level of granular security control for complex compliance needs. Azure Virtual Desktop (AVD) is a specialized solution for secure remote access rather than a primary hosting platform for the application itself.  YouTube +2 
    Comparison of Options 
    Feature  
    Azure App Service (PaaS) 
    Azure Virtual Machine (IaaS) 
    Azure Virtual Desktop (VDI) 
    Best For 
    Fast, lightweight deployment; low IT overhead. 
    Custom OS configs; full control over the stack. 
    Secure remote access for staff to a "cloud PC". 
    Affordability 
    Highest. Lower management costs; "Basic" plans start at ~$55/mo. 
    Medium. Pay-as-you-go; burstable (B-series) can be cheap but requires manual management. 
    Lowest. High costs due to multi-part billing (VM + Storage + User Licenses). 
    Security 
    Automated. Built-in patching and Azure-managed security. 
    Manual. Full control; you are responsible for OS patching and hardening. 
    Highest Access Security. Prevents data from leaving the cloud environment. 
    Complexity 
    Simple; "Web App + Database" setup is recommended for OpenEMR. 
    High; requires server admin skills to set up Linux/Windows, PHP, and MySQL. 
    Very High; involves host pools, workspace setup, and licensing. 
    Detailed Analysis 
    Most Affordable: Azure App Service (PaaS) 
    The Azure App Service is typically the most cost-effective for OpenEMR because it eliminates the need to pay for and manage an entire virtual server's OS. You can use the Azure Pricing Calculator to estimate costs for a "Web App + MySQL" configuration, which is the most lightweight method for running OpenEMR. 
    Most Secure: Azure Virtual Machine (IaaS) 
    While App Service is secure by default, an Azure Virtual Machine is the "most secure" choice only if you require highly specific security configurations or third-party security software that cannot run on a PaaS environment. For most healthcare providers, the managed security of App Service is sufficient and safer due to automated updates. 
    Special Case: Azure Virtual Desktop (AVD) 
    Azure Virtual Desktop is not typically used to host the OpenEMR web server. Instead, it is used by clinicians to access the EMR from a secure, remote desktop to ensure HIPAA-regulated data never touches their local, personal devices.  YouTube +4 
     
    I look forward to hearing more about the recommended setup and your quote for set up and management. 
     
    Best, 
     
     
    Delia Dura 
     
    Dura+Dura Co 
    Office (972) 502-9981 
    fax (972) 895-9232 
     
    Website :www.duraduraco.com
